<h3
id="ymusic-artist-bio-title">Biography</h3>








<p
id="artistPgBio">In
terms
of
sales
and
lasting
popularity,
Elton
John
was
the
biggest
pop
superstar
of
the
early
'70s.
Initially
marketed
as
a
singer/songwriter,
John
soon
revealed
he
could
craft
Beatlesque
pop
and
pound
out
rockers
with
equ...</p>
